<Text>Makes a very good salad, and they make it right in front of you exactly how you want it.

The price is a bit high, but if you think about what you're getting it's not too far off of the mark. The sandwiches are also good, but they don't shine quite as much as their salads do.

The service is slightly hit or miss, but generally not too bad, and the place is generally clean.

How busy it is, is really going to depend on when you go. If you're there outside of normal working folks' lunch hours, you can expect to order immediately and wait less than 10 minutes for your food, if you're there during the lunch rush ... good luck, it can be 30-45 from when you walk in the door to when you walk out with food, making it a viable option only for folks that eat fast AND work nearby AND have a full hour lunch.< /Text><Pics>None</Pics><Response>None<//Response>< gmapID>

< text>
I've eaten at many sandwich places in the Bay Area and Bianchini's is by far my favorite. Their sandwiches don't all use proprietary secret sauce like Ike's dirty sauce which, while heavenly on first consumption, eventually becomes tired and tends to make even very different sandwiches conform to a similar taste palette. Bianchini's sandwiches are no frills, good quality ingredients, and they have the tastiest bread with the best consistency I've found anywhere. The sandwiches taste fresh in a way that hard to qualify, and I never get tired of them. I must have ordered their number 1 a few dozen times and I still want more of it. I've only ordered a salad once, a chicken avocado salad with fruits and some kind of berry dressing, and that too was fantastic. Staff are friendly. I really can't recommend this place enough.< /text>

<review>I can highly recommend Orange Sky Adventures to anyone looking for a  intimate and authentic US travel experience, that the big-name tour companies just can't offer.  I was lucky enough to jump on Orange Sky's "Dirty South" tour in 2015, and it was by far the best tour experience of my life. Having done a fair bit of solo travel through the US, as well as a couple of Contiki tours, I had already crossed off a lot of the typical "touristy" locations, but I felt I had missed out on getting properly immersed in genuine American culture. Luckily Orange Sky was able to deliver this in spades!!

Driving through the back roads of the deep south, making pit stops at popular local restaurants and diners, the Orange Sky staff's local knowledge becomes very apparent. The selection of events and locations you visit along the way have all been carefully selected to give you a genuine insight into an array of American subcultures. <Rate>5</Rate>< Text>
Read closely because THIS TRIP IS BEST THING YOU WILL EVER DO IN THE USA/YOUR LIFE. This may sound like a big statement but it seriously is the most amazing trip and the only way to properly visit Yosemite. The best thing about Orange Sky Yosemite trip is exactly that, it feels so much more of a "road trip" than a "tour". Because there is so so many positive things to say about this trip, I'm going to narrow them down to just a few.

1) CONVENIENCE: this guy has thought of everything - sleeping bags, tents, pillows, camp fire, van with phone chargers, awesome country music playlist, car trip pillows and ridiculously amazing meals (French toast with strawberries for breakfast whilst camping whaaat?!).

2) LOCAL KNOWLEDGE: Dylan knows the best of the best. Yosemite is a seriously huge national park and it is impossible to see it all. So how do you know the best places to photograph and the hikes with the greatest views? He'll show you. He has made simple and easy to follow A4 maps that show the things you would want to see and has markings for trails, waterfalls, views, restrooms etc which is waaaay much easier than trying to figure out a map that is half the size of your body and has ridiculously small and unimportant information.

3) TIME: If you think you can see Yosemite in a day you are wrong. If you think you can see it in two days you are also wrong. What a lot of people don't realize about Yosemite is the amount of people that visit. The amount of people is generally fine, but what comes with a lot of people is a LOT of cars and I mean a lot. We drove in to the national park on a Saturday morning and the line of cars waiting to get into the car park would have been about 1.5-2 hour wait. And even in the afternoon the line up was just as bad. But Dylan has thought of it all and is able to significantly reduce the amount of time queueing so you don't have to sit impatiently in a mile long line of cars. Seriously this is such a time saver and you feel like a bad ass driving past all the queued cars. If you are thinking fine then I won't drive in a car and I will catch a bus works well think again, the lines for that are just as ridiculous. You're time in Yosemite will be 85% queuing/being frustrated and 15% sightseeing. Whilst with orange sky you will only be in the car for such a small time and so will be able to feel 100% happy about how much Yosemite you see.

3) SO MUCH FUN - Orange sky has such a fun, chilled and personal vibe. Dylan is so passionate and wise and made the whole trip amazing. My favourite parts other than the national park would have to be hanging out in the campsite, making smores and going to the river with everyone after a day's hike. Plus he knows so much about American food/history/states and will be answer all your questions like what's the ultimate thing to order at In and Out burger and what the best things to do in San Francisco are.

Orange sky provides the absolute BEST TIME and you are crazy if you think there is another way to experience Yosemite. It was definitely the favourite part of my holiday and I would do anything to go back!!! Don't miss out on this trip, there is absolutely no tour that will give you the same unreal experience.< /Text>

<text>Tours are like friends. A tour schedule too regimented and jam-packed is like going on vacation with that one dependable mate, who's always organised and got your back, but sometimes you'd swear they've got a stick up their butt. Often times this guy can leave you feeling rushed and stressed out.  On the other hand, too much freedom with insufficient guidance is like spending your whole afternoon sharing a blunt with your most mellow dank bro; you run the risk of wasting a lot of time and ending up not achieving all that you could.

On our trip with Orange Sky, our guide/spirit animal Dylan with his abundant experience working with major tour companies and relaxed southern mannerisms walked the fine line between these two extremes with ease. Whether you're with him for two days or three, Dylan has put careful consideration into selecting only the best that Yosemite has to offer so you won't miss a thing.

Orange Sky hooks you up with all your gear, solid grub, booze, country jams and a sweet ride around the park in Buddy, leaving you free to have a great time during the day absorbing the amazing surroundings and plenty of time at night to ponder the universes greater mysteries; like how Dylan can be so chill, yet at the same time so on top of things.

I'd definitely recommend taking the three day trip so you have more time to relax and also checking out the morbid but riveting annals of Deaths in Yosemite so you can learn how not to be stupid and fall off a waterfall and die.<//text><userid>108694681467464038451< /userid><Rate>5< /Rate>< Name>

< Review>
Dirty South 2015

From Nascar to college football to boot scootin' in Nashville, you're in for a whirlwind 12 days as you visit 6 different states. The Dirty South tour is the real deal, it's that authentic Southern Culture experience that blows your mind from start to finish. Everything they do down there is bigger and better. And what better way to immerse yourself, than with OrangeSky at the helm? You'll be hard pushed to find any other tour company around that can deliver this unique trip of a lifetime as good as OrangeSky can. There's really only one way to approach a trip like this, and that's with an open mind. The people, the music, the food and drink, the sport, try it all. If you're having any reservations, toss them aside and dive in, you won't regret it.

The entire trip was incredible, and it's hard to single any one thing out, but a particular highlight would have to be the Nascar at Talladega. I've never been a big motor sports fan, but Talladega is about more than just the race itself, it's the whole weekend event. Camping and partying with tens of thousands of fellow race fans and campers. Kicking back around your camp-fire, with a beer and a BBQ. There's an amazing vibe at Talladega, everyone's there for a good time and it's impossible not to. As for the actual race, this is something else, I was speechless once I saw the size of it, and the first time those 40 cars come hurtling passed at speeds of 320km/h is a moment I'll remember for the rest of my life.

Our tour guide Dylan, is very out going, professional and kept everything running smoothly and his vast knowledge of the south is seriously impressive. If you need anything, he'll sort it for you, he loves his job and what he does. Thanks for the best tour I've done, and will see you again for Dirty South 2016.<//Review>

<Date>1520303931545<//Date><Rating>5<//Rating>< Text>
This has always been a go-to for our family, but they changed recently and made it even better. Pork spring rolls with peanut sauce are wonderfully seasoned. Sound odd? Try them and you'll see what I mean. The Pho actually improved. Just when you think nothing could improve on an already complex flavored soup, they made that happen too. It is hard to pinpoint, but it's like they managed to add a slightly nutty profile that adds to the finish. Sesame perhaps? If you're a Pho fan and are in the AV or Bakersfield, make the trip. And, right after, check out the other destination location just south of there- Veritas Wine and Tapas. Tehachapi seems to have some real gems to offer.<//Text>

This last trip my husband and I  got marinated steak cubes and they were definitely between meh and bad. The spring rolls were awesome, and the shrimp fried rice was closer to good than meh. Beef noodle soup was also order and I thought the soup was great but the beef was kind of gross. It was as if a package of sliced roast beef was cut up and thrown it. My husband and I agreed on everything's rating except he didn't like the spring rolls. Since it is a smaller restaurant there was only one server and he played host, waiter, answered the phone and dealt with everything to do with to go orders except cooking the actual food while the kitchen staff seemed to be a lot less busy. We could tell by watching them come out of the kitchen, watch the server working hard doing everything, than lazily stroll back to the kitchen. We watched this happen several times and we weren't even there for a very long time. I get that kitchen staff shouldn't be assisting, but it's kind of a rude thing to do. Some cross training with someone from the kitchen who isn't doing much should be in order so that the server isn't running around crazy. We left our server a nice big tip because he definitely did everything to deserve it. With how meh the taste of the food was, the kitchen needs some serious retraining.<//text>< Pictures>

< review>
I drive by this store daily and occasionally stop by for Lotto.  Since the owner change over 2 years ago, they open early at 6am and stay open late, but I hardly ever see more than a couple of cars in the lot.  Maybe many people walk here.  I've seen some reviews raving about the freshly made sandwiches here, but I've never seen any customers at the deli or any employees working at the deli, which makes me wonder about the freshness of the sandwich ingredients.  Store appears to be family-run and friendly.  Store stocks a wide selection of beers & liquor and also has a lot of smoking and vaping paraphernalia.< /review>

< review>
My family and I had to choose a new optometry practice as our long-time optometrist moved out of state. We were very apprehensive about this process of choosing a new optometrist for our family. After researching online extensively and reading all the reviews, we decided on Westlake Vision Center Optometry for their high calibered optometrists and positive reviews.

Westlake Vision Center Optometry did not disappoint. We had the best optometry experience ever in our 35+ years of wearing glasses. Westlake Vision Optometry office is a most professional and family-friendly optometry office.

My family and I each saw a different optometrist in the Westlake Vision Optometry office: Dr. Yamada, Dr. Chen, and Dr. Sakata.  We compared notes and agreed that all three optometrists are excellent, knowledgeable and, experienced.  The optometrists all took the time to explain each step of the eye exam process, patiently answered any questions and/or concerns that we had,  used analogies we can understand, educated us on our eye care and eye exercises that we can do, and even informed us on the new developments and latest technology for eye care available.

We all had positive experiences from taking care of insurance matters before our scheduled appointments, to check-in with covid-19 precautionary measures and thorough eye exams, to selecting the right frames while taking into consideration our prescription, comfort, and how the frame fits on our faces. We did not feel rushed at all and appreciated being treated like a person, not a number to get in and out of the office despite the busyness of this office.

Anita, the office manager, is absolutely amazing and helpful.  She is very friendly, patient, and kind. Anita has the gift of hospitality to make you feel at ease and right at home. She took the time to help us select our frames after listening to our wish-list, and was able to select the most appropriate and pertinent frames. Once we selected our respective frames, she took the time to explain the insurance coverage and breakdown of our costs.

Our experience with our first contact with Westlake Vision Center Optometry to the end of our visit has been very smooth and enjoyable. We look forward to receiving our new prescription glasses soon!

If you are looking for a new vision provider, look no further! We highly recommend Westlake Vision Center Optometry as you will be impressed with the professional vision care at this office. We can tell you based on our own personal experience that the other positive reviews you have read are true!< /review>

<Review>I have been going Westlake Vision Center since I was 7 years old. My primary optometrist is Dr. Yamada, but sometimes I see Dr. Chen. Both doctors are incredible at what they do and ease into transition of each part of the appointment. The receptionists are also friendly, but often swamped with so much work. With that said, the reason why I knocked off one star is the overlap of appointments with other clients.

The last time I visited Westlake Vision Center, I had an appointment at 12 PM. However, I didn't actually see the optometrist until 12:45 PM when two clients that had the same time slot as me were seen ahead of me. There are only two appointment rooms, yet the receptionists overlap 2-3 people per time slot. In this case, expect to wait 30-60 min before seeing your optometrist; otherwise, you can always reschedule.

Parking near the optometrist is chaotic, especially when there are other stores nearby that people tend to frequent. If you don't mind the walk, park in the parking structure on the west side behind Home Depot.<//Review>< Pics>
